1) app/page.tsx – înlocuiește TOT fișierul cu acesta
"use client";

import dynamic from "next/dynamic";
import { useEffect, useState } from "react";

type Land = {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  locality: string;
  link: string;
  lat: number;
  lng: number;
  score: number;
  negotiatedPrice: number;
  confirmed: boolean; // ✅ NOU
};

const Map = dynamic(() => import("./map"), { ssr: false });

function uid() {
  return Math.random().toString(36).slice(2) + Date.now().toString(36);
}

const STORAGE_KEY = "terenuri_v1";

export default function Home() {
  const [lands, setLands] = useState<Land[]>([]);

  // ✅ 1) Ascultăm mutarea pinului (din map.tsx)
  useEffect(() => {
    function onMarkerMoved(e: any) {
      const { id, lat, lng } = e.detail || {};
      if (!id || typeof lat !== "number" || typeof lng !== "number") return;

      setLands((prev) =>
        prev.map((t) => (t.id === id ? { ...t, lat, lng } : t))
      );
    }

    window.addEventListener("markerMoved", onMarkerMoved);
    return () => window.removeEventListener("markerMoved", onMarkerMoved);
  }, []);

  // ✅ 2) Încărcare din localStorage la pornire
  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
      if (raw) {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);

        // „upgrade” sigur dacă ai date vechi fără confirmed
        const normalized: Land[] = Array.isArray(parsed)
          ? parsed.map((t: any) => ({
              id: String(t.id || uid()),
              title: String(t.title || "Teren nou"),
              locality: String(t.locality || ""),
              link: String(t.link || ""),
              lat: Number(t.lat ?? 45.9432),
              lng: Number(t.lng ?? 24.9668),
              score: Number(t.score ?? 0),
              negotiatedPrice: Number(t.negotiatedPrice ?? 0),
              confirmed: Boolean(t.confirmed ?? false),
            }))
          : [];

        setLands(normalized);
      } else {
        // seed de început
        setLands([
          {
            id: uid(),
            title: "Teren nou",
            locality: "Râmnicu Vâlcea",
            link: "https://exemplu.ro",
            lat: 45.0997,
            lng: 24.3693,
            score: 49,
            negotiatedPrice: 19000,
            confirmed: false,
          },
        ]);
      }
    } catch {
      // ignore
    }
  }, []);

  // ✅ 3) Salvare automată în localStorage la orice modificare
  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(lands));
    } catch {
      // ignore
    }
  }, [lands]);

  const onAdd = () => {
    setLands((prev) => [
      {
        id: uid(),
        title: "Teren nou",
        locality: "Timișoara",
        link: "https://exemplu.ro",
        lat: 45.7597,
        lng: 21.2300,
        score: 30,
        negotiatedPrice: 19000,
        confirmed: false,
      },
      ...prev,
    ]);
  };

  const onDelete = (id: string) => {
    setLands((prev) => prev.filter((t) => t.id !== id));
  };

  // ✅ Confirmă / Deblochează
  const onConfirm = (id: string) => {
    setLands((prev) =>
      prev.map((t) => (t.id === id ? { ...t, confirmed: true } : t))
    );
  };

  const onUnconfirm = (id: string) => {
    setLands((prev) =>
      prev.map((t) => (t.id === id ? { ...t, confirmed: false } : t))
    );
  };

  const fmt = (n: number) => {
    try {
      return new Intl.NumberFormat("ro-RO").format(n);
    } catch {
      return String(n);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ display: "flex", height: "100vh", width: "100vw" }}>
      {/* SIDEBAR */}
      <div
        style={{
          width: 360,
          background: "#0b0b0b",
          color: "white",
          padding: 14,
          overflow: "auto",
          borderRight: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.12)",
        }}
      >
        <div style={{ fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: 10 }}>Terenuri (V1)</div>

        <button
          onClick={onAdd}
          style={{
            width: "100%",
            padding: "10px 12px",
            borderRadius: 10,
            border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25)",
            background: "transparent",
            color: "white",
            cursor: "pointer",
            marginBottom: 14,
          }}
        >
          Adaugă teren
        </button>

        {lands.map((t) => (
          <div
            key={t.id}
            style={{
              border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.18)",
              borderRadius: 12,
              padding: 12,
              marginBottom: 12,
              background: "rgba(255,255,255,0.03)",
            }}
          >
            <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between" }}>
              <div style={{ fontWeight: 700 }}>{t.title}</div>
              <div style={{ opacity: 0.85 }}>Scor: {t.score}</div>
            </div>

            <div style={{ opacity: 0.9, marginTop: 4 }}>{t.locality}</div>

            <div style={{ opacity: 0.8, marginTop: 6, fontSize: 13 }}>
              Pret negociat: {fmt(t.negotiatedPrice)}
            </div>

            <div style={{ opacity: 0.85, marginTop: 8, fontSize: 13 }}>
              Status:{" "}
              {t.confirmed ? (
                <span style={{ color: "#7CFC00" }}>✅ Confirmat (pin blocat)</span>
              ) : (
                <span style={{ color: "#ffcc00" }}>⏳ Neconfirmat</span>
              )}
            </div>

            <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 10, marginTop: 10, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
              <a
                href={t.link}
                target="_blank"
                rel="noreferrer"
                style={{
                  padding: "8px 10px",
                  borderRadius: 10,
                  border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25)",
                  color: "white",
                  textDecoration: "none",
                  display: "inline-block",
                }}
              >
                Deschide anunț
              </a>

              {!t.confirmed ? (
                <button
                  onClick={() => onConfirm(t.id)}
                  style={{
                    padding: "8px 10px",
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25)",
                    background: "transparent",
                    color: "white",
                    cursor: "pointer",
                  }}
                >
                  Confirmă locația
                </button>
              ) : (
                <button
                  onClick={() => onUnconfirm(t.id)}
                  style={{
                    padding: "8px 10px",
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25)",
                    background: "transparent",
                    color: "white",
                    cursor: "pointer",
                  }}
                >
                  De-blochează
                </button>
              )}

              <button
                onClick={() => onDelete(t.id)}
                style={{
                  padding: "8px 10px",
                  borderRadius: 10,
                  border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25)",
                  background: "transparent",
                  color: "white",
                  cursor: "pointer",
                }}
              >
                Șterge
              </button>
            </div>

            <div style={{ marginTop: 10, fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>
              Trage pinul pe hartă, apoi apasă „Confirmă locația”.
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* MAP */}
      <div style={{ flex: 1, position: "relative" }}>
        <Map lands={lands} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
2) app/map.tsx – înlocuiește TOT fișierul cu acesta
"use client";

import "leaflet/dist/leaflet.css";
import { MapContainer, TileLayer, Marker, Popup } from "react-leaflet";
import L from "leaflet";

export type LandOnMap = {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  locality: string;
  link: string;
  lat: number;
  lng: number;
  score: number;
  negotiatedPrice: number;
  confirmed: boolean; // ✅ NOU
};

const markerIcon = new L.Icon({
  iconUrl: "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-icon.png",
  iconRetinaUrl: "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-icon-2x.png",
  shadowUrl: "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-shadow.png",
  iconSize: [25, 41],
  iconAnchor: [12, 41],
});

export default function Map({ lands = [] }: { lands: LandOnMap[] }) {
  return (
    <MapContainer
      center={[45.9432, 24.9668]}
      zoom={7}
      style={{ height: "100%", width: "100%" }}
    >
      <TileLayer
        attribution="&copy; OpenStreetMap contributors"
        url="https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png"
      />

      {lands.map((l) => (
        <Marker
          key={l.id}
          position={[l.lat, l.lng]}
          icon={markerIcon}
          draggable={!l.confirmed} // ✅ pin blocat dacă e confirmat
          eventHandlers={{
            dragend: (e) => {
              // dacă e confirmat, nu ar trebui să ajungă aici (draggable=false), dar lăsăm safe:
              if (l.confirmed) return;

              const p = (e.target as any).getLatLng();
              window.dispatchEvent(
                new CustomEvent("markerMoved", {
                  detail: { id: l.id, lat: p.lat, lng: p.lng },
                })
              );
            },
          }}
        >
          <Popup>
            <div style={{ minWidth: 240 }}>
              <div>
                <strong>{l.title}</strong>
              </div>
              <div>{l.locality}</div>
              <div>Scor: {l.score}</div>
              <div>Pret negociat: {Math.round(l.negotiatedPrice)}</div>

              <div style={{ marginTop: 8, fontSize: 13 }}>
                Status:{" "}
                {l.confirmed ? (
                  <span style={{ color: "#1fbf5b" }}>✅ Confirmat (pin blocat)</span>
                ) : (
                  <span style={{ color: "#ffcc00" }}>⏳ Neconfirmat</span>
                )}
              </div>

              <div style={{ marginTop: 8 }}>
                <a href={l.link} target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">
                  Deschide anunț
                </a>
              </div>

              <div style={{ marginTop: 8, fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>
                {l.confirmed
                  ? "Pinul este blocat. Apasă „De-blochează” în stânga ca să îl poți muta."
                  : "Trage pinul ca să salvezi coordonatele, apoi confirmă locația."}
              </div>
            </div>
          </Popup>
        </Marker>
      ))}
    </MapContainer>
  );
}

"use client";

import "leaflet/dist/leaflet.css";
import { MapContainer, TileLayer, Marker, Popup } from "react-leaflet";
import L from "leaflet";

export type LandOnMap = {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  locality: string;
  link: string;
  lat: number;
  lng: number;
  score: number;
  negotiatedPrice: number;
  confirmed?: boolean; // ✅ nou
};

const markerIcon = new L.Icon({
  iconUrl: "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-icon.png",
  iconRetinaUrl: "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-icon-2x.png",
  shadowUrl: "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-shadow.png",
  iconSize: [25, 41],
  iconAnchor: [12, 41],
});

export default function Map({ lands = [] }: { lands: LandOnMap[] }) {
  return (
    <MapContainer
      center={[45.9432, 24.9668]}
      zoom={7}
      style={{ height: "100%", width: "100%" }}
    >
      <TileLayer
        attribution="&copy; OpenStreetMap contributors"
        url="https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png"
      />

      {lands.map((l) => (
        <Marker
          key={l.id}
          position={[l.lat, l.lng]}
          icon={markerIcon}
          draggable={!l.confirmed} // ✅ blocat când confirmat
          eventHandlers={{
            dragend: (e) => {
              // dacă e confirmat, ignorăm (siguranță)
              if (l.confirmed) return;

              const p = (e.target as any).getLatLng();
              window.dispatchEvent(
                new CustomEvent("markerMoved", {
                  detail: { id: l.id, lat: p.lat, lng: p.lng },
                })
              );
            },
          }}
        >
          <Popup>
            <div style={{ minWidth: 220 }}>
              <div>
                <strong>{l.title}</strong>
              </div>
              <div>{l.locality}</div>
              <div>Scor: {l.score}</div>
              <div>Pret negociat: {Math.round(l.negotiatedPrice)}</div>

              <div style={{ marginTop: 6 }}>
                <a href={l.link} target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">
                  Deschide anunț
                </a>
              </div>

              <div style={{ marginTop: 6, fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>
                {l.confirmed
                  ? "Pin confirmat (blocat)."
                  : "Trage pinul ca să salvezi coordonatele."}
              </div>
            </div>
          </Popup>
        </Marker>
      ))}
    </MapContainer>
  );
}
2) page.tsx (buton Confirmă / De-blochează + status + salvare în localStorage)
Deschide app/page.tsx și fă 3 modificări:

A) În type Land adaugă confirmed?: boolean;
Caută type Land = { ... } și adaugă linia:

confirmed?: boolean;
B) În seed-ul inițial adaugă confirmed: false
În “seed de început”, în obiectul terenului, adaugă:

confirmed: false,
C) Adaugă funcțiile + UI pentru confirmare/deblocare
În Home() (sub onDelete de exemplu), pune:

const onConfirm = (id: string) => {
  setLands((prev) =>
    prev.map((t) => (t.id === id ? { ...t, confirmed: true } : t))
  );
};

const onUnconfirm = (id: string) => {
  setLands((prev) =>
    prev.map((t) => (t.id === id ? { ...t, confirmed: false } : t))
  );
};
Apoi, în card-ul fiecărui teren (în lands.map((t) => (...) )), unde ai butoanele, adaugă și:

status linie

buton confirmă / deblochează

Exemplu (în interiorul cardului, înainte de butoane, sau după “Pret negociat”):

<div style={{ marginTop: 6, fontSize: 13 }}>
  Status:{" "}
  {t.confirmed ? (
    <span style={{ color: "#1fbf5b" }}>✅ Confirmat (pin blocat)</span>
  ) : (
    <span style={{ color: "#ffcc00" }}>⏳ Neconfirmat</span>
  )}
</div>
Și în zona cu butoane (unde ai “Deschide anunț” și “Șterge”), adaugă butonul 3:

{t.confirmed ? (
  <button
    onClick={() => onUnconfirm(t.id)}
    style={{
      padding: "8px 10px",
      borderRadius: 10,
      border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25)",
      background: "transparent",
      color: "white",
      cursor: "pointer",
    }}
  >
    De-blochează
  </button>
) : (
  <button
    onClick={() => onConfirm(t.id)}
    style={{
      padding: "8px 10px",
      borderRadius: 10,
      border: "1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.25)",
      background: "transparent",
      color: "white",
      cursor: "pointer",
    }}
  >
    Confirmă locația
  </button>
)}
Gata — asta e “implementarea completă”.

În browser: http://localhost:3000

Trage pinul → se mută ✅

Apasă Confirmă locația → pinul NU mai e dragabil ✅

Refresh (F5) → rămâne confirmat ✅

Apasă De-blochează → pinul devine iar dragabil ✅

Mai jos ai pas cu pas exact ce faci pentru Pasul 5 (Editare teren), fără să te încurci.

1) Deschide fișierul corect

app → page.tsx (click pe el)

2) Adaugă “selectedLandId” (în page.tsx)

Imediat sub el, adaugă:

const [selectedLandId, setSelectedLandId] = useState<string | null>(null);
3) Creează “selectedLand”
Tot în page.tsx, sub state-uri, adaugă:

const selectedLand = lands.find(l => l.id === selectedLandId) || null;
4) Când apeși pe un teren din listă → îl selectezi

5) La formular: în loc să editezi direct l, editezi selectedLand

Regula:

dacă selectedLand e null, afișezi un mesaj: “Selectează un teren din listă”.

Exemplu (pui deasupra formularului):

if (!selectedLand) {
  return <div style={{ padding: 12 }}>Selectează un teren din listă.</div>;
}
6) Ca să edităm, facem o funcție “updateLand”
În page.tsx, adaugă funcția asta (sub selectedLand):

function updateLand(id: string, patch: Partial<any>) {
  setLands(prev =>
    prev.map(l => (l.id === id ? { ...l, ...patch } : l))
  );
}
Apoi, în input-uri, faci așa:

<input
  value={selectedLand.title}
  onChange={(e) => updateLand(selectedLand.id, { title: e.target.value })}
/>
(la fel pentru locality, price, link, score)

{lands.map((t) => (
  <div>
    ...
  </div>

1) Înlocuiește TOT în app/page.tsx
Deschide app/page.tsx → Ctrl+A → Delete → lipește:

"use client";

import dynamic from "next/dynamic";
import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";

type Land = {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  locality: string;
  link: string;
  lat: number;
  lng: number;
  score: number;
  negotiatedPrice: number;
  confirmed: boolean; // ✅ pin blocat
};

const Map = dynamic(() => import("./map"), { ssr: false });

const STORAGE_KEY = "terenuri_v1";

function uid() {
  return Math.random().toString(36).slice(2) + Date.now().toString(36);
}

function safeNumber(v: any, fallback: number) {
  const n = Number(v);
  return Number.isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
}

export default function Home() {
  const [lands, setLands] = useState<Land[]>([]);
  const [selectedLandId, setSelectedLandId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const selectedLand = useMemo(() => {
    return lands.find((l) => l.id === selectedLandId) || null;
  }, [lands, selectedLandId]);

  // 1) Load din localStorage (la start)
  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
      if (raw) {
        const parsed = JSON.parse(raw);

        if (Array.isArray(parsed)) {
          const normalized: Land[] = parsed.map((t: any) => ({
            id: String(t.id ?? uid()),
            title: String(t.title ?? "Teren nou"),
            locality: String(t.locality ?? "Timișoara"),
            link: String(t.link ?? ""),
            lat: safeNumber(t.lat, 45.75797),
            lng: safeNumber(t.lng, 21.22898),
            score: safeNumber(t.score, 30),
            negotiatedPrice: safeNumber(t.negotiatedPrice, 19000),
            confirmed: Boolean(t.confirmed ?? false),
          }));

          setLands(normalized);
          if (normalized.length > 0) setSelectedLandId(normalized[0].id);
          return;
        }
      }
    } catch {
      // ignore
    }

    // seed de început (dacă nu există nimic salvat)
    const seed: Land[] = [
      {
        id: uid(),
        title: "Teren nou",
        locality: "Timișoara",
        link: "https://exemplu.ro",
        lat: 45.75797,
        lng: 21.22898,
        score: 30,
        negotiatedPrice: 19000,
        confirmed: false,
      },
      {
        id: uid(),
        title: "Teren nou",
        locality: "Timișoara",
        link: "https://exemplu.ro",
        lat: 45.7597,
        lng: 21.23,
        score: 30,
        negotiatedPrice: 19000,
        confirmed: false,
      },
    ];

    setLands(seed);
    setSelectedLandId(seed[0].id);
  }, []);

  // 2) Save automat la orice modificare
  useEffect(() => {
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(lands));
    } catch {
      // ignore
    }
  }, [lands]);

  // 3) Ascultăm mutarea pinului (din map.tsx)
  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = (e: Event) => {
      const ce = e as CustomEvent;
      const detail = ce.detail as { id: string; lat: number; lng: number } | undefined;
      if (!detail) return;

      setLands((prev) =>
        prev.map((t) => (t.id === detail.id ? { ...t, lat: detail.lat, lng: detail.lng } : t))
      );
    };

    window.addEventListener("markerMoved", handler as EventListener);
    return () => window.removeEventListener("markerMoved", handler as EventListener);
  }, []);

  const onAdd = () => {
    const item: Land = {
      id: uid(),
      title: "Teren nou",
      locality: "Timișoara",
      link: "https://exemplu.ro",
      lat: 45.75797,
      lng: 21.22898,
      score: 30,
      negotiatedPrice: 19000,
      confirmed: false,
    };

    setLands((prev) => [item, ...prev]);
    setSelectedLandId(item.id);
  };

  const onDelete = (id: string) => {
    setLands((prev) => prev.filter((t) => t.id !== id));
    setSelectedLandId((cur) => (cur === id ? null : cur));
  };

  const onConfirm = (id: string) => {
    setLands((prev) => prev.map((t) => (t.id === id ? { ...t, confirmed: true } : t)));
  };

  const onUnconfirm = (id: string) => {
    setLands((prev) => prev.map((t) => (t.id === id ? { ...t, confirmed: false } : t)));
  };

  const updateSelected = (patch: Partial<Land>) => {
    if (!selectedLandId) return;
    setLands((prev) => prev.map((t) => (t.id === selectedLandId ? { ...t, ...patch } : t)));
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ display: "flex", height: "100vh", overflow: "hidden" }}>
      {/* SIDEBAR */}
      <div
        style={{
          width: 360,
          background: "#111",
          color: "#fff",
          padding: 12,
          overflowY: "auto",
          borderRight: "1px solid #222",
        }}
      >
        <div style={{ fontWeight: 800, fontSize: 18, marginBottom: 10 }}>Terenuri (V1)</div>

        <button
          onClick={onAdd}
          style={{
            width: "100%",
            padding: "10px 12px",
            borderRadius: 10,
            border: "1px solid #333",
            background: "#0b0b0b",
            color: "#fff",
            cursor: "pointer",
            marginBottom: 12,
          }}
        >
          Adaugă teren
        </button>

        {lands.map((l) => {
          const isSelected = l.id === selectedLandId;

          return (
            <div
              key={l.id}
              onClick={() => setSelectedLandId(l.id)}
              style={{
                border: isSelected ? "1px solid #5aa9ff" : "1px solid #333",
                borderRadius: 12,
                padding: 12,
                marginBottom: 10,
                background: isSelected ? "#141a22" : "#0d0d0d",
                cursor: "pointer",
              }}
            >
              <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", gap: 10 }}>
                <div style={{ fontWeight: 800 }}>{l.title}</div>
                <div style={{ opacity: 0.9 }}>Scor: {l.score}</div>
              </div>

              <div style={{ opacity: 0.9, marginTop: 6 }}>{l.locality}</div>
              <div style={{ opacity: 0.9, marginTop: 6 }}>Preț negociat: {l.negotiatedPrice}</div>

              <div style={{ marginTop: 6 }}>
                Status:{" "}
                {l.confirmed ? (
                  <span style={{ color: "#1fbf5b" }}>✅ Confirmat</span>
                ) : (
                  <span style={{ color: "#ffcc00" }}>⏳ Neconfirmat</span>
                )}
              </div>

              <div style={{ display: "flex", gap: 8, marginTop: 10, flexWrap: "wrap" }}>
                <button
                  onClick={(e) => {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    if (l.link) window.open(l.link, "_blank", "noreferrer");
                  }}
                  style={{
                    padding: "8px 10px",
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    border: "1px solid #333",
                    background: "#0b0b0b",
                    color: "#fff",
                    cursor: "pointer",
                  }}
                >
                  Deschide anunț
                </button>

                {l.confirmed ? (
                  <button
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      onUnconfirm(l.id);
                    }}
                    style={{
                      padding: "8px 10px",
                      borderRadius: 10,
                      border: "1px solid #333",
                      background: "#0b0b0b",
                      color: "#fff",
                      cursor: "pointer",
                    }}
                  >
                    Deblochează
                  </button>
                ) : (
                  <button
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      onConfirm(l.id);
                    }}
                    style={{
                      padding: "8px 10px",
                      borderRadius: 10,
                      border: "1px solid #333",
                      background: "#0b0b0b",
                      color: "#fff",
                      cursor: "pointer",
                    }}
                  >
                    Confirmă locația
                  </button>
                )}

                <button
                  onClick={(e) => {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    onDelete(l.id);
                  }}
                  style={{
                    padding: "8px 10px",
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    border: "1px solid #333",
                    background: "#0b0b0b",
                    color: "#fff",
                    cursor: "pointer",
                  }}
                >
                  Șterge
                </button>
              </div>

              {!l.confirmed && (
                <div style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.7, marginTop: 10 }}>
                  Trage pinul pe hartă, apoi apasă „Confirmă locația”.
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          );
        })}

        {/* FORM EDITARE (Pas 5) */}
        <div style={{ marginTop: 14, paddingTop: 14, borderTop: "1px solid #222" }}>
          <div style={{ fontWeight: 800, marginBottom: 8 }}>Editare teren selectat</div>

          {!selectedLand ? (
            <div style={{ opacity: 0.8 }}>Selectează un teren din listă.</div>
          ) : (
            <div style={{ display: "grid", gap: 8 }}>
              <label style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>Titlu</label>
              <input
                value={selectedLand.title}
                onChange={(e) => updateSelected({ title: e.target.value })}
                style={{
                  padding: 10,
                  borderRadius: 10,
                  border: "1px solid #333",
                  background: "#0b0b0b",
                  color: "#fff",
                }}
              />

              <label style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>Localitate</label>
              <input
                value={selectedLand.locality}
                onChange={(e) => updateSelected({ locality: e.target.value })}
                style={{
                  padding: 10,
                  borderRadius: 10,
                  border: "1px solid #333",
                  background: "#0b0b0b",
                  color: "#fff",
                }}
              />

              <label style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>Link</label>
              <input
                value={selectedLand.link}
                onChange={(e) => updateSelected({ link: e.target.value })}
                style={{
                  padding: 10,
                  borderRadius: 10,
                  border: "1px solid #333",
                  background: "#0b0b0b",
                  color: "#fff",
                }}
              />

              <label style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>Preț negociat</label>
              <input
                type="number"
                value={selectedLand.negotiatedPrice}
                onChange={(e) => updateSelected({ negotiatedPrice: safeNumber(e.target.value, 0) })}
                style={{
                  padding: 10,
                  borderRadius: 10,
                  border: "1px solid #333",
                  background: "#0b0b0b",
                  color: "#fff",
                }}
              />

              <label style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.8 }}>Scor</label>
              <input
                type="number"
                value={selectedLand.score}
                onChange={(e) => updateSelected({ score: safeNumber(e.target.value, 0) })}
                style={{
                  padding: 10,
                  borderRadius: 10,
                  border: "1px solid #333",
                  background: "#0b0b0b",
                  color: "#fff",
                }}
              />

              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, opacity: 0.7, marginTop: 6 }}>
                Coordonate: {selectedLand.lat.toFixed(6)}, {selectedLand.lng.toFixed(6)}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* HARTA */}
      <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
        <Map lands={lands} selectedLandId={selectedLandId} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
2) Înlocuiește TOT în app/map.tsx
Deschide app/map.tsx → Ctrl+A → Delete → lipește:

"use client";

import "leaflet/dist/leaflet.css";
import L from "leaflet";
import { MapContainer, Marker, TileLayer } from "react-leaflet";

type LandOnMap = {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  locality: string;
  link: string;
  lat: number;
  lng: number;
  score: number;
  negotiatedPrice: number;
  confirmed: boolean;
};

const icon = new L.Icon({
  iconUrl:
    "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-icon.png",
  iconRetinaUrl:
    "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-icon-2x.png",
  shadowUrl:
    "https://unpkg.com/leaflet@1.9.4/dist/images/marker-shadow.png",
  iconSize: [25, 41],
  iconAnchor: [12, 41],
});

export default function Map({
  lands = [],
  selectedLandId,
}: {
  lands: LandOnMap[];
  selectedLandId: string | null;
}) {
  const center: [number, number] = [45.75797, 21.22898];

  return (
    <MapContainer
      center={center}
      zoom={10}
      style={{ height: "100vh", width: "100%" }}
    >
      <TileLayer
        attribution='&copy; OpenStreetMap contributors'
        url="https://{s}.tile.openstreetmap.org/{z}/{x}/{y}.png"
      />

      {lands.map((l) => (
        <Marker
          key={l.id}
          position={[l.lat, l.lng]}
          icon={icon}
          draggable={!l.confirmed}
          eventHandlers={{
            dragend: (e) => {
              const marker = e.target;
              const pos = marker.getLatLng();

              window.dispatchEvent(
                new CustomEvent("markerMoved", {
                  detail: { id: l.id, lat: pos.lat, lng: pos.lng },
                })
              );
            },
          }}
        />
      ))}
    </MapContainer>
  );
}

B) Adaugă 2 iconițe (normal + selectat)
În map.tsx, după importuri (sau la începutul fișierului), adaugă:

const normalIcon = L.divIcon({
  className: "",
  html: `<div style="
    width:14px;height:14px;border-radius:999px;
    background:#2b6cb0;border:2px solid white;
    box-shadow:0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,.35);
  "></div>`,
  iconSize: [14, 14],
  iconAnchor: [7, 7],
});

const selectedIcon = L.divIcon({
  className: "",
  html: `<div style="
    width:18px;height:18px;border-radius:999px;
    background:#f59e0b;border:3px solid white;
    box-shadow:0 3px 10px rgba(0,0,0,.45);
  "></div>`,

C) La fiecare Marker: icon diferit + click = select
Unde faci marker-ele cu lands.map(...), la <Marker ...>:

Pune icon-ul:

icon={l.id === selectedLandId ? selectedIcon : normalIcon}
Pune click-ul:

eventHandlers={{
  click: () => onSelectLand?.(l.id),
}}
Exemplu (schelet):

<Marker
  position={[l.lat, l.lng]}
  draggable
  icon={l.id === selectedLandId ? selectedIcon : normalIcon}
  eventHandlers={{
    click: () => onSelectLand?.(l.id),
    // păstrezi aici și ce aveai deja pentru drag/move
  }}
>
D) Zoom automat pe terenul selectat (sigur, fără să strice)
În map.tsx adaugă componenta asta (deasupra return-ului sau oriunde în fișier):

function FlyToSelected({
  selected,
}: {
  selected: { lat: number; lng: number } | null;
}) {
  const map = useMap();

  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!selected) return;
    map.flyTo([selected.lat, selected.lng], Math.max(map.getZoom(), 13), {
      duration: 0.6,
    });
  }, [selected, map]);

  return null;
}
⚠️ Dacă nu ai useMap importat, adaugă la import:

import { MapContainer, TileLayer, Marker, useMap } from "react-leaflet";
și dacă nu ai React importat, pune sus:

import React from "react";
Apoi, în JSX-ul hărții (în interiorul <MapContainer ...>), pune:

<FlyToSelected
  selected={
    selectedLandId
      ? lands.find((x) => x.id === selectedLandId) ?? null
      : null
  }
/>
